  (S
    (NP (DT The) (NN government))
    (VP
      (MD will)
      (VP
        (VB confer)
        (NP
          (CD four)
          (NML
            (NML (NNP Padma) (NNP Vibhushan))
            (CC and)
            (NML (CD fourteen) (NNP Padma) (NNP Bhushan)))
          (NNS awards))
        (NP (DT this) (NN year))))
    (. .)))
